- The benzoyl part has a hydroxyl and chlorine on the ring.
- The aniline part (amide nitrogen connected to the second ring) has chlorine and nitro substituents.

### Step 2: Identify Key Functional Groups and Structural Features
Key features that might influence the property include:
- **Hydroxyl group (phenol)**: Often contributes to polarity and hydrogen bonding, which can affect properties like solubility or bioactivity.

- **Amide bond**: Polar group, capable of hydrogen bonding, often associated with specific interactions in biological or physical properties.
- **Nitro group**: Strong electron-withdrawing group, increases polarity, and can impact electronic properties of the molecule.
